                                    1163      63.     Ÿ     ********************************************************        Ÿ
                                    1164      64.     Ÿ                                                                     Ÿ
                                    1165      65.     Ÿ   Parameters                                                        Ÿ
                                    1166      66.     Ÿ                                                                     Ÿ
                                    1167      67.     Ÿ    VOLS=nn         Number of ddcards to process, a number           Ÿ
                                    1168      68.     Ÿ                    starting at 00 and incremented by 1 is           Ÿ
                                    1169      69.     Ÿ                    appended to a four character ddname stem to      Ÿ
                                    1170      70.     Ÿ                    form the ddname used for formatting or           Ÿ
                                    1171      71.     Ÿ                    restoring.                                       Ÿ
                                    1172      72.     Ÿ                                                                     Ÿ
                                    1173      73.     Ÿ    DDNAME=xxxx     Four character DD name stem to be used for       Ÿ
                                    1174      74.     Ÿ                    formatting or restore data definitions.          Ÿ
                                    1175      75.     Ÿ                                                                     Ÿ
                                    1176      76.     Ÿ    BLKSIZE=nnnn    Blocksize used for formatting, defaults          Ÿ
                                    1177      77.     Ÿ                    TO 2048 FOR ORVYL FILES AND 4096 FOR             Ÿ
                                    1178      78.     Ÿ                    page data sets.                                  Ÿ
                                    1179      79.     Ÿ                                                                     Ÿ
                                    1180      80.     Ÿ                    Note:  this may or may not                       Ÿ
                                    1181      81.     Ÿ                           equal the data set blksize which          Ÿ
                                    1182      82.     Ÿ                           includes the file header except when      Ÿ
                                    1183      83.     Ÿ                           the header is                             Ÿ
                                    1184      84.     Ÿ                           contained in the record key field.        Ÿ
                                    1185      85.     Ÿ                                                                     Ÿ
                                    1186      86.     Ÿ    (NO)FDC         Format a file directory bitmap and               Ÿ
                                    1187      87.     Ÿ                    catalog.                                         Ÿ
                                    1188      88.     Ÿ                                                                     Ÿ
                                    1189      89.     Ÿ    (NO)PAGE        Format an Orvyl page file.                       Ÿ
                                    1190      90.     Ÿ                                                                     Ÿ
                                    1191      91.     Ÿ    (NO)CYLINDER    Data set must be allocated on cylinder           Ÿ
                                    1192      92.     Ÿ                    boundaries.                                      Ÿ
                                    1193      93.     Ÿ                                                                     Ÿ
                                    1194      94.     Ÿ    CONTIGUOUS      Data set must be one extent.                     Ÿ
                                    1195      95.     Ÿ                                                                     Ÿ
                                    1196      96.     Ÿ    (NO)CNTG        Data set may have more than one extent.          Ÿ
                                    1197      97.     Ÿ                                                                     Ÿ
                                    1198      98.     Ÿ    (NO)RESTORE     Perform a restore operation,  The input          Ÿ
                                    1199      99.     Ÿ                    data is defined by the "DUMPTAPE" DD card.       Ÿ
                                    1200     100.     Ÿ                                                                     Ÿ
                                                      ¾þþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþ»

 0016C6                            13103  1 1581.                END    ,                 OF FILE NODE = FULL BLK
                                   13107  1 1582.     *   A balanced node must have at least 3 entrys for collapse to work
                                   13108  1 1583.     * right.  In order to use the average of the nodes being balanced
                                   13109  1 1584.     * as a sufficient indicator for not having to collapse, a limit
                                   13110  1 1585.     * must be placed on the maximum size of an entry.
                                   13111  1 1586.     *   Worst case is 3 nodes, 2 of which have 3 entrys, and the other node
                                   13112  1 1587.     * having only 2 entrys.  This would cause a failure if the average
                                   13113  1 1588.     * space of these entrys >= max free space allowed per node (total
                                   13114  1 1589.     * space >= 3 times the max free space per node).  Therefore the limit
                                   13115  1 1590.     * imposed is: max entry < 3/8 of max free space per node (that 8 entrys
                                   13116  1 1591.     * of max size cannot have a total size >= 3 times the max free space
                                   13117  1 1592.     * per node).
